	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading mw-first-heading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">Item</span></h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="vector-body">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From League of Legends Wiki, LoL Wiki</div>
		<div id="contentSub"><div id="mw-content-subtitle"></div></div>
		<div id="contentSub2"></div>
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" lang="en" dir="ltr"><noscript><iframe src="https://www.googletagmanager.com/ns.html?id=GTM-MVJGX7KS" height="0" width="0" style="display:none;visibility:hidden"></iframe></noscript><div class="mw-parser-output"><div id="game-nav" class="noexcerpt noprint onlymobile navigation-not-searchable wiki-namespace-btns"><div data-type="lol" data-page="Item" class="game-nav-item game-nav-item-active" style="display:inline-block; position:relative; height:60px; width:60px"><span class="game-nav-item-select" style="position:absolute"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/LoR:Items" title="LoR:Item"><img alt="LoR:Item" src="/en-us/images/Select_icon_nav.svg?b145d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="60" height="60" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="512" /></a></span></span><span style="position:absolute; top:15px; left:16px"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/LoR:Items" title="LoR:Item"><img alt="LoR:Item" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Legends_of_Runeterra_icon_nav.png/28px-Legends_of_Runeterra_icon_nav.png?c2707" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="28" height="34" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Legends_of_Runeterra_icon_nav.png?c2707 2x" data-file-width="43" data-file-height="52" /></a></span></span></div><div data-type="wr" data-page="WR:Item" class="game-nav-item" style="display:inline-block; position:relative; height:60px; width:60px"><span class="game-nav-item-select" style="position:absolute"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/WR:Item" title="WR:Item"><img alt="WR:Item" src="/en-us/images/Select_icon_nav.svg?b145d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="60" height="60" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="512" /></a></span></span><span style="position:absolute; top:15px; left:15px"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/WR:Item" title="WR:Item"><img alt="WR:Item" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Wild_Rift_icon_nav.png/32px-Wild_Rift_icon_nav.png?173d1" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="32" height="26" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/Wild_Rift_icon_nav.png?173d1 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="52" /></a></span></span></div></div>
<figure typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/en-us/File:Shopkeeper_Preseason_2021_Promo_01.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Shopkeeper_Preseason_2021_Promo_01.jpg/400px-Shopkeeper_Preseason_2021_Promo_01.jpg?71a76" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="400" height="225" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Shopkeeper_Preseason_2021_Promo_01.jpg/800px-Shopkeeper_Preseason_2021_Promo_01.jpg?71a76 2x" data-file-width="1814" data-file-height="1020" /></a><figcaption>Summoner's Rift <a href="/en-us/Universe:Yordle" title="Universe:Yordle">yordle</a> shopkeeper presenting <a href="/en-us/Season_2021" title="Season 2021">Season 2021</a> items. Various <a href="/en-us/Champions" class="mw-redirect" title="Champions">champions</a> can be seen behind the shopkeeper.</figcaption></figure>
<p>An <b>item</b> is a modular enhancement that grants bonuses and capabilities beyond what <a href="/en-us/Champion" title="Champion">champions</a> have access to by default. Most <b>items</b> can be purchased from the <a href="/en-us/Shop" title="Shop">shop</a> in exchange for <span class="inline-image label-after" style="display:inline;color:#E2BA3D;white-space:pre;text-shadow:-1px 0 black,0 1px black,1px 0 black,0 -1px black;" data-param=""><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Gold" title="An icon representing Gold"><img alt="An icon representing Gold" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/20px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/40px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991 2x" data-file-width="96" data-file-height="96" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;">gold</span></span> while near the <a href="/en-us/Spawn" title="Spawn">spawn</a>, while a small number of them may be distributed to players from various effects.
</p><p>In League of Legends, acquiring an item is the same as equipping it and its <a href="/en-us/Stat" class="mw-redirect" title="Stat">stats</a> and effects are gained <i>passively</i>. A number of items may additionally feature unique <a href="/en-us/Active_ability_items" title="Active ability items">active item abilities</a> that can be used via the respective slot's <a href="/en-us/Hotkey" class="mw-redirect" title="Hotkey">hotkey</a> and are highlighted by a gold trim on the HUD.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Acquiring_items">Acquiring items</span></h2>
<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/en-us/File:Item_shop_desk.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Item_shop_desk.jpg/300px-Item_shop_desk.jpg?28490" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="300" height="155" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Item_shop_desk.jpg/600px-Item_shop_desk.jpg?28490 2x" data-file-width="1600" data-file-height="829" /></a><figcaption>Items and gold.</figcaption></figure>
<p>The right side of the player's HUD displays a <span class="inline-image label-after" style="display:inline;color:#E2BA3D;white-space:pre;text-shadow:-1px 0 black,0 1px black,1px 0 black,0 -1px black;" data-param=""><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Gold" title="An icon representing Gold"><img alt="An icon representing Gold" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/20px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/40px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991 2x" data-file-width="96" data-file-height="96" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Gold" title="Gold">gold</a></span></span> counter, the <a href="/en-us/Shop#Item_queuing" title="Shop">item queue</a> circle, and the player's <b>inventory</b> where items are placed. The inventory has six slots: this limitation renders their combination and order—known as the player's <i>build</i>—an important factor in determining champion power and agency. A seventh, <i>trinket slot</i> is occupied by <i><a href="/en-us/Trinket_item" title="Trinket item">trinket items</a></i>. Players are usually given a default trinket item upon starting the game, which may be temporarily or permanently swapped with other trinket items throughout the game. The inventory, excluding the trinket, can be rearranged by <span class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Hotkeys" title="Left Mouse Button"><img alt="Left Mouse Button" src="/en-us/images/LMB.svg?00ea5" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="13" height="20" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="300" /></a></span> clicking-and-dragging on items' icons; if an item occupies the target slot, the dragged item and the target will simply exchange slots.
</p><p>Items can be acquired in two ways:
</p>
<ol><li>By <b>purchasing</b> them from the <a href="/en-us/Shop" title="Shop">shop</a> while within valid range of the shopkeeper's stall—the gold counter button lights up while in range. The shop interface is accessed by <span class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Hotkeys" title="Left Mouse Button"><img alt="Left Mouse Button" src="/en-us/images/LMB.svg?00ea5" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="13" height="20" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="300" /></a></span> clicking on the model of the ally team's shopkeeper stall, <span class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Hotkeys" title="Left Mouse Button"><img alt="Left Mouse Button" src="/en-us/images/LMB.svg?00ea5" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="13" height="20" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="300" /></a></span> clicking on the gold counter in the HUD, or using the assigned hotkey (default <span class="template_sbc"><b>P</b></span>). The shop is located right next to the <a href="/en-us/Spawn" title="Spawn">spawn platform</a> (fountain) in most maps.</li>
<li>Through the process of <b>distribution</b>. Distributed items are acquired upon fulfilling a condition, varying by item, and they automatically go into the next available slot in the inventory. Champions can acquire distributed items while at any location, they do not need to be in the shop's range.</li></ol>
<p>Items that the champion cannot equip due to any restrictions will feature a <span typeof="mw:File"><span title="Icon in the shop for locked items (items that the player cannot purchase)"><img alt="Icon in the shop for locked items (items that the player cannot purchase)" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Shop_item_lock.png/20px-Shop_item_lock.png?700ba" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Shop_item_lock.png/40px-Shop_item_lock.png?700ba 2x" data-file-width="48" data-file-height="48" /></span></span> lock icon in the shop.
</p>
<figure class="mw-halign-center" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/en-us/File:Item_shop_interface.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Item_shop_interface.png/500px-Item_shop_interface.png?d1d09" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="500" height="302" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Item_shop_interface.png/1000px-Item_shop_interface.png?d1d09 2x" data-file-width="1598" data-file-height="965" /></a><figcaption>The item shop interface.</figcaption></figure>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Effects">Effects</span></h2>
<figure class="mw-halign-right" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/en-us/File:Item_key_bindings.png" class="mw-file-description"><img src="/en-us/images/Item_key_bindings.png?5d536" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="266" height="143" class="mw-file-element" data-file-width="266" data-file-height="143" /></a><figcaption>Items that include effects the player can actively use are highlighted with a golden trim (shown: <span class="template_sbc"><b>2</b></span>, <span class="template_sbc"><b>3</b></span> and <span class="template_sbc"><b>4</b></span>).</figcaption></figure>
<p>Most items passively provide power or effects upon being equipped, but some items may feature an <i>active ability</i> (shortened to "active").
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">Stats</a></b>. The majority of items provide a number of <a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">stats</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/en-us/Passive" title="Passive">Passive item abilities</a></b> grant a special effect automatically.</li>
<li><b><a href="/en-us/Active_ability_items" title="Active ability items">Active item abilities</a></b> and <a href="/en-us/Consumable_item" title="Consumable item">consumables</a> grant a special effect upon <i>cast</i>, by clicking on the item or by pressing their slot's designated <a href="/en-us/Hotkey" class="mw-redirect" title="Hotkey">hotkey</a>. Item actives are distinct active spells from <a href="/en-us/Champion_ability" title="Champion ability">champion abilities</a>, while consumables grant lesser, beneficial effects.</li>
<li><b><a href="/en-us/Aura" title="Aura">Auras</a></b> are <a href="/en-us/Buff" title="Buff">buffs</a> (positive effects) or <a href="/en-us/Debuff" title="Debuff">debuffs</a> (negative effects) that may passively affect nearby allied or enemy units, respectively.</li></ul>
<p>Like champion abilities, item abilities may be <a href="/en-us/Named_item_effect" title="Named item effect">named</a> and have certain <a href="/en-us/Targeting" title="Targeting">targeting</a>, <a href="/en-us/Range" title="Range">ranges</a>, <a href="/en-us/Cooldown" title="Cooldown">cooldowns</a> or other special conditions. Item effects' cooldown is affected by <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Ability_haste" title="Ability haste"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Cooldown_reduction_icon.png/15px-Cooldown_reduction_icon.png?27276" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Cooldown_reduction_icon.png/30px-Cooldown_reduction_icon.png?27276 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/en-us/Item_haste" class="mw-redirect" title="Item haste">item haste</a></span> and is shown on their icon while incurred.
</p><p>Items that grant static permanent stat bonuses via an item effect (e.g. <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Rod of Ages" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Rod_of_Ages" title="An icon for the item Rod of Ages"><img alt="An icon for the item Rod of Ages" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Rod_of_Ages_item.png/20px-Rod_of_Ages_item.png?2e093" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Rod_of_Ages_item.png/40px-Rod_of_Ages_item.png?2e093 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Rod_of_Ages" title="Rod of Ages">Rod of Ages</a></span></span>) will have that bonus added to the innate stats. This does not only apply to the display of stats that the item grants: the item effects' bonuses count as innate stats themselves. Notably, <span class="inline-image label-after rune-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-rune="Jack of All Trades" data-game="lol"><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Jack_of_All_Trades" title="An icon representing Jack of All Trades"><img alt="An icon representing Jack of All Trades" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Jack_of_All_Trades_rune.png/20px-Jack_of_All_Trades_rune.png?c9838" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Jack_of_All_Trades_rune.png/40px-Jack_of_All_Trades_rune.png?c9838 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="word-break: keep-all;"><a href="/en-us/Jack_of_All_Trades" title="Jack of All Trades">Jack of All Trades</a></span></span> counts these bonuses as if they were innate to the item, thus granting a stack of the rune if the stat is unique.
</p><p>The icon of certain items in the inventory may be accompanied by a counter. Items that utilize a <a href="/en-us/Ammunition" title="Ammunition">stock</a> always display their number of available charges and become greyed out to indicate when no charges are available. Items that grant a <a href="/en-us/Stack" title="Stack">stacking</a> bonus or have a requirement may display a counter which indicates the granted bonus or remaining amount.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Classification">Classification</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quality_tiers"><span id="Quality_Tiers"></span>Quality tiers</span></h3>
<p>Items are primarily categorized into quality tiers. Starter-tier items are meant to grant a modest amount of power at the start of the game and players are recommended to spend their starting <span class="inline-image label-after" style="display:inline;color:#E2BA3D;white-space:pre;text-shadow:-1px 0 black,0 1px black,1px 0 black,0 -1px black;" data-param=""><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Gold" title="An icon representing Gold"><img alt="An icon representing Gold" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/20px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/40px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991 2x" data-file-width="96" data-file-height="96" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;">gold</span></span> on them. Basic- and Epic-tier items on the other hand may be combined in <b>recipes</b> to build powerful Legendary-tier items.
</p>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/Starter_item" title="Starter item">Starter</a></dt>
<dd>These items are effective at the beginning of the game, but their value diminishes as the game goes on since they only grant moderate power compared to other items. Most starter items are not part of recipes and therefore cannot build into higher-tier items, occupying a slot in the player's inventory until sold.</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/Basic_item" title="Basic item">Basic</a></dt>
<dd>These items provide a single stat.</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/Epic_item" title="Epic item">Epic</a></dt>
<dd>These items may provide higher stats than basic items and/or new effects. Some Epic items offer a lesser version of the Legendary item(s) that they build into.</dd></dl>
<dl><dt><a href="/en-us/Legendary_item" title="Legendary item">Legendary</a></dt>
<dd>Combining Basic and Epic items makes Legendary items, which provide the greatest power and effects of all items.</dd></dl>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Boots"><span id="Boot"></span><span id="Boot_tiers"></span>Boots</span></h3>
<p>Boots are a distinct ecosystem of items. Only one Boots item can be equipped that will give champions important <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/15px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/30px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed"><i>flat</i> movement speed</a></span>, but these items may also grant other <a href="/en-us/Champion_statistic" title="Champion statistic">stats</a> or <a href="/en-us/Named_item_effect" title="Named item effect">effects</a>, similar to regular items.
</p><p>Boots items have three tiers, with each higher tier strictly granting more innate <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/15px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Movement_speed_icon.png/30px-Movement_speed_icon.png?f928e 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/en-us/Movement_speed" title="Movement speed">movement speed</a></span> than the lower tier.
</p>
<ul><li>Tier 1: The baseline is <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal">25 innate movement speed</span>. This tier contains <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Boots" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Boots" title="An icon for the item Boots"><img alt="An icon for the item Boots" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Boots_item.png/20px-Boots_item.png?1e048" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Boots_item.png/40px-Boots_item.png?1e048 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Boots" title="Boots">Boots</a></span></span> (and similar strength boot items e.g. <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Slightly Magical Boots" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Slightly_Magical_Boots" title="An icon for the item Slightly Magical Boots"><img alt="An icon for the item Slightly Magical Boots" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Slightly_Magical_Boots_item.png/20px-Slightly_Magical_Boots_item.png?c1989" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Slightly_Magical_Boots_item.png/40px-Slightly_Magical_Boots_item.png?c1989 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Slightly_Magical_Boots" title="Slightly Magical Boots">Slightly Magical Boots</a></span></span>).</li>
<li>Tier 2: Purchased upgrades of Tier 1 boots. The baseline is <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal">45 innate movement speed</span>. They are always available for purchase and automatically become <b>Triumphant</b>, gaining a small bonus, upon a team earning the <a href="/en-us/Feats_of_Strength" title="Feats of Strength"><i>Blessing of Noxus</i></a>.</li>
<li>Tier 3: Purchased upgrades of Tier 2 boots. The baseline is <span style="color: #9FFF4D; white-space:normal">50 innate movement speed</span>. They only become available for purchase after the team has earned the <i>Blessing of Noxus</i> and owns at least two Legendary-tier items.</li></ul>
<p>Note that <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Symbiotic Soles" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Symbiotic_Soles" title="An icon for the item Symbiotic Soles"><img alt="An icon for the item Symbiotic Soles" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Symbiotic_Soles_item.png/20px-Symbiotic_Soles_item.png?7f173" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Symbiotic_Soles_item.png/40px-Symbiotic_Soles_item.png?7f173 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Symbiotic_Soles" title="Symbiotic Soles">Symbiotic Soles</a></span></span> and <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Synchronized Souls" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Synchronized_Souls" title="An icon for the item Synchronized Souls"><img alt="An icon for the item Synchronized Souls" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Synchronized_Souls_item.png/20px-Synchronized_Souls_item.png?9c23b" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Synchronized_Souls_item.png/40px-Synchronized_Souls_item.png?9c23b 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Synchronized_Souls" title="Synchronized Souls">Synchronized Souls</a></span></span> are both tier <b>2</b> boots, because they are both part of the <a href="/en-us/Named_item_effect#Symbiosis" title="Named item effect">Symbiosis</a> quest.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Consumables">Consumables</span></h3>
<dl><dd><i><div class="dablink">Main article: <a href="/en-us/Consumable_item" title="Consumable item">Consumable item</a></div></i></dd></dl>
<p>Consumable items grant small or moderate beneficial and utility effects. Some trinket items are also consumables. They are highlighted on the HUD similar to items that feature active abilities, since they can also be used.
</p><p>The player may be allowed to purchase certain consumables multiple times, up to a limit, which will then occupy only one slot together. Some consumables are removed from the inventory upon use while others may feature <a href="/en-us/Ammunition" title="Ammunition">charges</a> that are replenished passively, upon fulfilling a certain condition, or upon re-visiting the shop.
</p><p>Certain consumable items are automatically consumed if acquired while the inventory is full, granting their effects immediately and removing the item from the inventory. <span class="inline-image label-after spell-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-spell="Recall" data-game="lol"><span class="border icon-20" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Recall" title="An icon representing Recall"><img alt="An icon representing Recall" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Recall.png/20px-Recall.png?cfc4d" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Recall.png/40px-Recall.png?cfc4d 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Recall" title="Recall">Recall</a></span></span> is not interrupted by activating a consumable item (with the exception of <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Eye of the Herald" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Eye_of_the_Herald" title="An icon for the item Eye of the Herald"><img alt="An icon for the item Eye of the Herald" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Eye_of_the_Herald_item.png/20px-Eye_of_the_Herald_item.png?22971" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Eye_of_the_Herald_item.png/40px-Eye_of_the_Herald_item.png?22971 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Eye_of_the_Herald" title="Eye of the Herald">Eye of the Herald</a></span></span>).
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Transformation">Transformation</span></h2>
<p>Most items can be combined by paying the cost in <span class="inline-image label-after" style="display:inline;color:#E2BA3D;white-space:pre;text-shadow:-1px 0 black,0 1px black,1px 0 black,0 -1px black;" data-param=""><span style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Gold" title="An icon representing Gold"><img alt="An icon representing Gold" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/20px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Gold_colored_icon.png/40px-Gold_colored_icon.png?39991 2x" data-file-width="96" data-file-height="96" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;">gold</span></span>. Some, however, cannot be purchased and are obtained solely through the process of <b>transformation</b> that occurs under a specific condition. That condition is usually gaining a specified amount of <b>stacks</b> for the item or completing an explicit <b>quest</b>. Certain transforming items, such as <a href="/en-us/Named_item_effect#Support_Quest" title="Named item effect">Support Quest</a> items, may feature more than one transformation.
</p><p>Transformations happen automatically upon fulfilling the condition, even outside of the shop, granting their stats and/or effects immediately and replacing the lesser item with the transformed one in the inventory.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Uniqueness">Uniqueness</span></h2>
<p>Items and their effects may be <i>unique</i>, which encompasses the following rules for how their effects may (or may not) function together, or upon player's purchases.
</p>
<ul><li>By default, only one of each Legendary-tier item may be equipped.</li>
<li><b><a href="/en-us/Named_item_effect#Isolated_effects" title="Named item effect">Single effect limitations</a></b> prevent the item's effect from <a href="/en-us/Stack" title="Stack">stacking</a> by equipping more than one of that same item. A unique effect can only be gained once.</li>
<li><b><a href="/en-us/Named_item_effect#Shared_effects" title="Named item effect">Shared effect limitations</a></b> broaden the constraint of unique effects to <i>different items</i> instead of only the same item. These unique effects can only be gained once from all items that share it, even if the two items seem to be entirely unrelated.</li>
<li><b><a href="/en-us/Item_group" title="Item group">Item group</a> limitations</b> prohibit equipping more than one item within the same group, <span typeof="mw:File"><span title="Icon in the shop for locked items (items that the player cannot purchase)"><img alt="Icon in the shop for locked items (items that the player cannot purchase)" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Shop_item_lock.png/20px-Shop_item_lock.png?700ba" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Shop_item_lock.png/40px-Shop_item_lock.png?700ba 2x" data-file-width="48" data-file-height="48" /></span></span> <i>locking</i> the player out from equipping further members. This excludes acquiring an item within the group by combining its recipe or via transformation—both processes instantly override the item in the player's inventory and thus avoid the limitation.</li>
<li>All buff or debuff <a href="/en-us/Aura" title="Aura">auras</a> can only affect a unit once. Damaging auras may be able to stack, affecting all units within.</li></ul>
<p>If an effect features a cooldown and more than one of the item can be equipped, any other equipped item that has the same named effect will share the cooldown, even if not specifically used.
</p><p>Items do not possess uniqueness by default. In the case of <b>all</b> Legendary items as well as <b>most</b> consumable items however, intentionally strict and artificial rules are implemented to prevent the player from equipping or incurring more than one of the same effect simultaneously, compel diversity in item builds, and reduce waste of value.
</p><p>Internally, item uniqueness is handled by both general cases and name &amp; group ID tags.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notifications">Notifications</span></h2>
<p><span class="template_sbc"><b>Potion Highlights:</b></span> This applies to players at <a href="/en-us/Experience_(summoner)" title="Experience (summoner)">account levels</a> 1–10. If their champion drops under <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Health" title="Health"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Health_icon.png/15px-Health_icon.png?f8c57" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="15" height="15" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Health_icon.png/30px-Health_icon.png?f8c57 2x" data-file-width="72" data-file-height="72" /></a></span>&#160;<span style="color: #21B053; white-space:normal">40% <b>maximum</b> health</span></span> and is <a href="/en-us/Combat_status" title="Combat status">out-of-combat</a>, the icon of any health-restoring consumables will flash.
</p><p><span class="template_sbc"><b>Shop Reminder:</b></span> The shop button will flash upon exiting the shop area without spending the given starting gold.
</p><p>On <span class="glossary" style="white-space:pre; position:relative;" data-game="lol" data-tip="Summoner&#39;s rift"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Summoner%27s_Rift" title="Summoner&#39;s Rift"><img src="/en-us/images/thumb/Summoner%27s_Rift_icon.png/20px-Summoner%27s_Rift_icon.png?7a043" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Summoner%27s_Rift_icon.png/40px-Summoner%27s_Rift_icon.png?7a043 2x" data-file-width="100" data-file-height="100" /></a></span> <a href="/en-us/Summoner%27s_Rift" title="Summoner&#39;s Rift">Summoner's Rift</a></span>, exiting the base without a <a href="/en-us/Trinket_item" title="Trinket item">trinket</a> will automatically grant <span class="inline-image item-icon label-after item-icon" style="display:inline;white-space:pre;" data-param="" data-item="Stealth Ward" data-game="lol"><span class="border" style="display:inline-block;position:relative;" data-width="20"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/en-us/Stealth_Ward" title="An icon for the item Stealth Ward"><img alt="An icon for the item Stealth Ward" src="/en-us/images/thumb/Stealth_Ward_item.png/20px-Stealth_Ward_item.png?7cccb" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="20" height="20" class="mw-file-element" srcset="/en-us/images/thumb/Stealth_Ward_item.png/40px-Stealth_Ward_item.png?7cccb 2x" data-file-width="64" data-file-height="64" /></a></span></span> <span style="white-space:normal;"><a href="/en-us/Stealth_Ward" title="Stealth Ward">Stealth Ward</a></span></span>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span></h2>
<ul><li>Items are usually weapons, artifacts and other objects from the canon <a href="/en-us/Universe:Runeterra" title="Universe:Runeterra">Runeterra</a> lore/background and are usually themed around a speciifc in-universe <a href="/en-us/Category:Places" title="Category:Places">region</a>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span></h2>
